+import torch
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+M = 64
+N = 64
+K = 16
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def test_kernel(A: S.Tensor((M, K), S.bf16), B: S.Tensor((K, N), S.bf16), C: S.Tensor((M, N), S.f32)):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // 64
+    lane = tid % 64
+    warp_row = warp_id // 2
+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+    lane_lo = lane % 32
+    lane_hi = lane // 32
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, S.convert(M * K * 2, S.i32))
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B, S.convert(K * N * 2, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    a_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    c_tile = S.make_shared((M, N), S.f32)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    if tid < 128:
+        load_idx = tid
+        load_row = load_idx % 64
+        seg = load_idx // 64
+        a_row_block = load_row // 32
+        a_row_lane = load_row % 32
+        a_off = S.convert((load_row * K + seg * 8) * 2, S.i32)
+        x_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_off, 0)
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane, seg * 2 + 0] = x_pack[0]
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane, seg * 2 + 1] = x_pack[1]
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 0] = x_pack[2]
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 1] = x_pack[3]
+    else:
+        load_idx = tid - 128
+        k_local = load_idx // 8
+        seg = load_idx % 8
+        b_col_block = seg // 4
+        b_seg_in_block = seg % 4
+        b_off = S.convert((k_local * N + b_col_block * 32 + b_seg_in_block * 8) * 2, S.i32)
+        w_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_off, 0)
+        k_half = k_local // 8
+        k_lane = k_local % 8
+        lane0 = (b_seg_in_block * 2 + 0) + k_lane * 8
+        lane1 = (b_seg_in_block * 2 + 1) + k_lane * 8
+        b_words[b_col_block, lane0, k_half * 2 + 0] = w_pack[0]
+        b_words[b_col_block, lane0, k_half * 2 + 1] = w_pack[1]
+        b_words[b_col_block, lane1, k_half * 2 + 0] = w_pack[2]
+        b_words[b_col_block, lane1, k_half * 2 + 1] = w_pack[3]
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    m_a = S.view(a_words[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(b_words[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)
+
+    local_col = warp_col * 32 + lane_lo
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        local_row = warp_row * 32 + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_hi + (acc_idx % 4)
+        c_tile[local_row, local_col] = c_lane[acc_idx]
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if tid < 64:
+        for j in S.range(64):
+            C[tid, j] = c_tile[tid, j]
+
+
+def main():
+    torch.manual_seed(0)
+    A = torch.randn((M, K), device="cuda", dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+    B = torch.randn((K, N), device="cuda", dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+    C = torch.zeros((M, N), device="cuda", dtype=torch.float32)
+    test_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (256, 1, 1))](A, B, C)
+    ref = A.float() @ B.float()
+    d = (C - ref).abs()
+    print("max", d.max().item(), "mean", d.mean().item())
+    print("row0_ref", ref[0, :16].cpu().tolist())
+    print("row0_got", C[0, :16].cpu().tolist())
+    print("row1_ref", ref[1, :16].cpu().tolist())
+    print("row1_got", C[1, :16].cpu().tolist())
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+        b_words[b_col_block, lane0, k_half * 2 + 0] = w_pack[0]
+        b_words[b_col_block, lane0, k_half * 2 + 1] = w_pack[1]
+        b_words[b_col_block, lane1, k_half * 2 + 0] = w_pack[2]
+        b_words[b_col_block, lane1, k_half * 2 + 1] = w_pack[3]
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    m_a = S.view(a_words[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(b_words[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)
+
+    local_col = warp_col * 32 + lane_lo
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        local_row = warp_row * 32 + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_hi + (acc_idx % 4)
+        c_tile[local_row, local_col] = c_lane[acc_idx]
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if tid < 64:
+        for j in S.range(64):
+            C[tid, j] = c_tile[tid, j]
+
+
+def main():
+    torch.manual_seed(0)
+    A = torch.randn((M, K), device="cuda", dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+    B = torch.randn((K, N), device="cuda", dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+    C = torch.zeros((M, N), device="cuda", dtype=torch.float32)
+    test_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (256, 1, 1))](A, B, C)
+    ref = A.float() @ B.float()
+    d = (C - ref).abs()
+    print("max", d.max().item(), "mean", d.mean().item())
+    print("row0_ref", ref[0, :16].cpu().tolist())
+    print("row0_got", C[0, :16].cpu().tolist())
+    print("row1_ref", ref[1, :16].cpu().tolist())
+    print("row1_got", C[1, :16].cpu().tolist())
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import unittest

import torch

from substrate_kernels import amdgpu_gemm_fast


class TestGEMM(unittest.TestCase):
    def setUp(self):
        """Set up test fixtures before each test method."""
        torch.manual_seed(0)
        self.rtol = 1e-2
        self.atol = 1e-3

    def test_gemm_1stage(self):
        m = 1024
        n = 1024
        k = 1024
        A = torch.randn((m, k), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
        B = torch.randn((k, n), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
        B_t = B.t().contiguous()
        expected = (A @ B).to(dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cpu")
        C = amdgpu_gemm_fast.gemm_1stage_pipeline_transposed_b(A, B_t)

        actual = C.to("cpu")

        # with open("gemm_1stage_pipeline_output.txt", "w") as f:
        #     f.write("Expected:\n")
        #     for i in range(m):
        #         row = expected[i].to(torch.float32)
        #         line = ''.join(f"{x:8.3f}" for x in row)
        #         f.write(f"{line}\n")

        #     f.write("\nActual:\n")
        #     for i in range(m):
        #         row = actual[i].to(torch.float32)
        #         line = ''.join(f"{x:8.3f}" for x in row)
        #         f.write(f"{line}\n")

        self.assertTrue(
            torch.allclose(actual, expected, rtol=self.rtol, atol=self.atol),
            msg=f"GEMM results do not match.\nExpected:\n{expected}\nActual:\n{actual}\n"
            f"Max absolute difference: {torch.max(torch.abs(actual - expected))}",
        )


if __name__ == "__main__":
    unittest.main()

+            self._cached_bias = bias.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()

+import torch
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+M = 64
+N = 64
+K = 16
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def test_kernel(A: S.Tensor((M, K), S.bf16), B: S.Tensor((K, N), S.bf16), C: S.Tensor((M, N), S.f32)):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // 64
+    lane = tid % 64
+    warp_row = warp_id // 2
+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+    lane_lo = lane % 32
+    lane_hi = lane // 32
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, S.convert(M * K * 2, S.i32))
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B, S.convert(K * N * 2, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    a_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    c_tile = S.make_shared((M, N), S.f32)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    if tid < 128:
+        load_idx = tid
+        load_row = load_idx % 64
+        seg = load_idx // 64
+        a_row_block = load_row // 32
+        a_row_lane = load_row % 32
+        a_off = S.convert((load_row * K + seg * 8) * 2, S.i32)
+        x_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_off, 0)
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane, seg * 2 + 0] = x_pack[0]
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane, seg * 2 + 1] = x_pack[1]
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 0] = x_pack[2]
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 1] = x_pack[3]
+    else:
+        load_idx = tid - 128
+        k_local = load_idx // 8
+        seg = load_idx % 8
+        b_col_block = seg // 4
+        b_seg_in_block = seg % 4
+        b_off = S.convert((k_local * N + b_col_block * 32 + b_seg_in_block * 8) * 2, S.i32)
+        w_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_off, 0)
+        k_half = k_local // 8
+        k_lane = k_local % 8
+        lane0 = (b_seg_in_block * 2 + 0) + k_lane * 8
+        lane1 = (b_seg_in_block * 2 + 1) + k_lane * 8
+        b_words[b_col_block, lane0, k_half * 2 + 0] = w_pack[0]
+        b_words[b_col_block, lane0, k_half * 2 + 1] = w_pack[1]
+        b_words[b_col_block, lane1, k_half * 2 + 0] = w_pack[2]
+        b_words[b_col_block, lane1, k_half * 2 + 1] = w_pack[3]
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    m_a = S.view(a_words[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(b_words[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)
+
+    local_col = warp_col * 32 + lane_lo
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        local_row = warp_row * 32 + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_hi + (acc_idx % 4)
+        c_tile[local_row, local_col] = c_lane[acc_idx]
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if tid < 64:
+        for j in S.range(64):
+            C[tid, j] = c_tile[tid, j]
+
+
+def main():
+    torch.manual_seed(0)
+    A = torch.randn((M, K), device="cuda", dtype=torch.bfloat16)

+    C = torch.zeros((M, N), device="cuda", dtype=torch.float32)

+    print("row1_ref", ref[1, :16].cpu().tolist())
+    print("row1_got", C[1, :16].cpu().tolist())
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp_id // 2
+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+    lane_lo = lane % 32
+    lane_hi = lane // 32
+    row_block = S.block_id(0)
+    row_base = row_block * BLOCK_ROWS
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_words = S.make_shared((2, WAVE_SIZE, 4), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((2, WAVE_SIZE, 4), S.u32)
+    c_tile = S.make_shared((BLOCK_ROWS, BLOCK_COLS), S.f32)
+    row_max = S.make_shared((BLOCK_ROWS,), S.f32)
+
+    neg_inf = S.convert(-1.0e30, S.f32)
+    if tid < BLOCK_ROWS:
+        row_max[tid] = neg_inf
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    for col_tile in S.range(COL_TILES):
+        c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+        col_base = col_tile * BLOCK_COLS
+
+        for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+            k_base = k_tile * BLOCK_K

+                a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 0] = x_pack[2]
+                a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 1] = x_pack[3]
+            else:

+                b_words[b_col_block, lane1, k_half * 2 + 1] = w_pack[3]

+class ModelNew(nn.Module):
     def __init__(self, in_features, out_features, pool_kernel_size, scale_factor):
         super().__init__()

+        self._cached_weight = None
+        self._cached_bias = None
+        self._cache_key = None
 
+    def _get_cached_params(self, x: torch.Tensor):
+        weight = self.matmul.weight
+        bias = self.matmul.bias
+        key = (
+            weight.data_ptr(),
+            bias.data_ptr(),
+            x.device,
+            x.dtype,
+        )
+        if self._cache_key != key:
+            self._cached_weight = weight.t().to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
+            self._cached_bias = bias.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
+            self._cache_key = key
+        return self._cached_weight, self._cached_bias

+import torch
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+M = 64
+N = 64
+K = 16
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def test_kernel(A: S.Tensor((M, K), S.bf16), B: S.Tensor((K, N), S.bf16), C: S.Tensor((M, N), S.f32)):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // 64
+    lane = tid % 64
+    warp_row = warp_id // 2
+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+    lane_lo = lane % 32
+    lane_hi = lane // 32
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, S.convert(M * K * 2, S.i32))
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B, S.convert(K * N * 2, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    a_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    c_tile = S.make_shared((M, N), S.f32)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    if tid < 128:
+        load_idx = tid
+        load_row = load_idx % 64
+        seg = load_idx // 64
+        a_row_block = load_row // 32
+        a_row_lane = load_row % 32
+        a_off = S.convert((load_row * K + seg * 8) * 2, S.i32)
+        x_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_off, 0)
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane, seg * 2 + 0] = x_pack[0]
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane, seg * 2 + 1] = x_pack[1]
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 0] = x_pack[2]
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 1] = x_pack[3]
+    else:
+        load_idx = tid - 128
+        k_local = load_idx // 8
+        seg = load_idx % 8
+        b_col_block = seg // 4
+        b_seg_in_block = seg % 4
+        b_off = S.convert((k_local * N + b_col_block * 32 + b_seg_in_block * 8) * 2, S.i32)
+        w_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_off, 0)
+        k_half = k_local // 8
+        k_lane = k_local % 8
+        lane0 = (b_seg_in_block * 2 + 0) + k_lane * 8
+        lane1 = (b_seg_in_block * 2 + 1) + k_lane * 8
+        b_words[b_col_block, lane0, k_half * 2 + 0] = w_pack[0]
+        b_words[b_col_block, lane0, k_half * 2 + 1] = w_pack[1]
+        b_words[b_col_block, lane1, k_half * 2 + 0] = w_pack[2]
+        b_words[b_col_block, lane1, k_half * 2 + 1] = w_pack[3]
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    m_a = S.view(a_words[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(b_words[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)
+
+    local_col = warp_col * 32 + lane_lo
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        local_row = warp_row * 32 + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_hi + (acc_idx % 4)
+        c_tile[local_row, local_col] = c_lane[acc_idx]
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if tid < 64:
+        for j in S.range(64):
+            C[tid, j] = c_tile[tid, j]
+
+
+def main():
+    torch.manual_seed(0)
+    A = torch.randn((M, K), device="cuda", dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+    B = torch.randn((K, N), device="cuda", dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+    C = torch.zeros((M, N), device="cuda", dtype=torch.float32)
+    test_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (256, 1, 1))](A, B, C)
+    ref = A.float() @ B.float()
+    d = (C - ref).abs()
+    print("max", d.max().item(), "mean", d.mean().item())
+    print("row0_ref", ref[0, :16].cpu().tolist())
+    print("row0_got", C[0, :16].cpu().tolist())
+    print("row1_ref", ref[1, :16].cpu().tolist())
+    print("row1_got", C[1, :16].cpu().tolist())
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

codex
The remaining plausible structural mistake is the B layout itself. I’m testing the transposed-B packing pattern that the local AMD GEMM pipeline examples are built around.

+BLOCK_ROWS = 64

+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4

+        bias = self.matmul.bias
+        key = (
+            weight.data_ptr(),
+            bias.data_ptr(),
+            x.device,
+            x.dtype,
+        )
+        if self._cache_key != key:
+            self._cached_weight = weight.t().to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
+            self._cached_bias = bias.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
+            self._cache_key = key
+        return self._cached_weight, self._cached_bias

+import torch
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+M = 64
+N = 64
+K = 16
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def test_kernel(A: S.Tensor((M, K), S.bf16), B: S.Tensor((N, K), S.bf16), C: S.Tensor((M, N), S.f32)):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // 64
+    lane = tid % 64
+    warp_row = warp_id // 2
+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+    lane_lo = lane % 32
+    lane_hi = lane // 32
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, S.convert(M * K * 2, S.i32))
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B, S.convert(K * N * 2, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    a_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    c_tile = S.make_shared((M, N), S.f32)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    if tid < 128:
+        load_idx = tid
+        load_row = load_idx % 64
+        seg = load_idx // 64
+        a_row_block = load_row // 32
+        a_row_lane = load_row % 32
+        a_off = S.convert((load_row * K + seg * 8) * 2, S.i32)
+        x_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_off, 0)
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane, seg * 2 + 0] = x_pack[0]
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane, seg * 2 + 1] = x_pack[1]
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 0] = x_pack[2]
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 1] = x_pack[3]
+    else:
+        load_idx = tid - 128
+        load_col = load_idx % 64
+        seg = load_idx // 64
+        b_col_block = load_col // 32
+        b_col_lane = load_col % 32
+        b_off = S.convert((load_col * K + seg * 8) * 2, S.i32)
+        w_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_off, 0)
+        b_words[b_col_block, b_col_lane, seg * 2 + 0] = w_pack[0]
+        b_words[b_col_block, b_col_lane, seg * 2 + 1] = w_pack[1]
+        b_words[b_col_block, b_col_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 0] = w_pack[2]
+        b_words[b_col_block, b_col_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 1] = w_pack[3]
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    m_a = S.view(a_words[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(b_words[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)
+
+    local_col = warp_col * 32 + lane_lo
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        local_row = warp_row * 32 + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_hi + (acc_idx % 4)
+        c_tile[local_row, local_col] = c_lane[acc_idx]
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if tid < 64:
+        for j in S.range(64):
+            C[tid, j] = c_tile[tid, j]
+
+
+def main():
+    torch.manual_seed(0)
+    A = torch.randn((M, K), device="cuda", dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+    B = torch.randn((K, N), device="cuda", dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+    B_t = B.t().contiguous()
+    C = torch.zeros((M, N), device="cuda", dtype=torch.float32)
+    test_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (256, 1, 1))](A, B_t, C)
+    ref = A.float() @ B.float()
+    d = (C - ref).abs()
+    print("max", d.max().item(), "mean", d.mean().item())
+    print("row0_ref", ref[0, :16].cpu().tolist())
+    print("row0_got", C[0, :16].cpu().tolist())
+    print("row1_ref", ref[1, :16].cpu().tolist())
+    print("row1_got", C[1, :16].cpu().tolist())
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+WAVE_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = 4
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+ROW_BLOCKS = BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_ROWS
+COL_TILES = OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_COLS
+K_TILES = IN_FEATURES // BLOCK_K
+
+X_NUM_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2
+W_NUM_BYTES = IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2
+
+
+def _launch():
+    return ((ROW_BLOCKS, 1, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp_id // 2
+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+    lane_lo = lane % 32
+    lane_hi = lane // 32
+    row_block = S.block_id(0)
+    row_base = row_block * BLOCK_ROWS
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(X_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_words = S.make_shared((2, WAVE_SIZE, 4), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((2, WAVE_SIZE, 4), S.u32)
+    c_tile = S.make_shared((BLOCK_ROWS, BLOCK_COLS), S.f32)
+    row_max = S.make_shared((BLOCK_ROWS,), S.f32)
+
+    neg_inf = S.convert(-1.0e30, S.f32)
+    if tid < BLOCK_ROWS:
+        row_max[tid] = neg_inf
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    for col_tile in S.range(COL_TILES):
+        c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+        col_base = col_tile * BLOCK_COLS
+
+        for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+            k_base = k_tile * BLOCK_K
 
-class ModelNew(nn.Module):
+            if tid < 128:
+                load_idx = tid
+                load_row = load_idx % BLOCK_ROWS
+                seg = load_idx // BLOCK_ROWS
+                a_row_block = load_row // 32
+                a_row_lane = load_row % 32
+                x_row = row_base + load_row
+                x_col = k_base + seg * 8
+                x_off = S.convert((x_row * IN_FEATURES + x_col) * 2, S.i32)
+                x_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, x_off, 0)
 
+                a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane, seg * 2 + 0] = x_pack[0]
+                a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane, seg * 2 + 1] = x_pack[1]
+                a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 0] = x_pack[2]
+                a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 1] = x_pack[3]
+            else:
+                load_idx = tid - 128
+                k_local = load_idx // 8
+                seg = load_idx % 8
+                b_col_block = seg // 4
+                b_seg_in_block = seg % 4
+                w_col = col_base + b_col_block * 32 + b_seg_in_block * 8
+                w_row = k_base + k_local
+                w_off = S.convert((w_row * OUT_FEATURES + w_col) * 2, S.i32)
+                w_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, w_off, 0)
+
+                k_half = k_local // 8
+                k_lane = k_local % 8
+                lane0 = k_lane + (b_seg_in_block * 2 + 0) * 8
+                lane1 = k_lane + (b_seg_in_block * 2 + 1) * 8
+                b_words[b_col_block, lane0, k_half * 2 + 0] = w_pack[0]
+                b_words[b_col_block, lane0, k_half * 2 + 1] = w_pack[1]
+                b_words[b_col_block, lane1, k_half * 2 + 0] = w_pack[2]
+                b_words[b_col_block, lane1, k_half * 2 + 1] = w_pack[3]
+
+            S.syncthreads()
+
+            m_a = S.view(a_words[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+            m_b = S.view(b_words[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+            c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+            c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)
+            S.syncthreads()
+
+        local_col = warp_col * 32 + lane_lo
+        for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+            local_row = warp_row * 32 + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_hi + (acc_idx % 4)
+            c_tile[local_row, local_col] = c_lane[acc_idx]
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        if tid < BLOCK_ROWS:
+            row = tid
+            for group in S.range(BLOCK_COLS // POOL_KERNEL_SIZE):
+                total = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+                group_col = col_base + group * POOL_KERNEL_SIZE
+                for t in S.range(POOL_KERNEL_SIZE):
+                    col = group * POOL_KERNEL_SIZE + t
+                    total += c_tile[row, col] + S.convert(BIAS0[group_col + t], S.f32)
+                v = total / S.convert(POOL_KERNEL_SIZE, S.f32)
+                v = S.convert(0.5, S.f32) * v * (
+                    S.convert(1.0, S.f32) + S.erf(v / S.convert(SQRT_2, S.f32))
+                )
+                v = v * S.convert(SCALE_FACTOR, S.f32)
+                if v > row_max[row]:
+                    row_max[row] = v
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    if tid < BLOCK_ROWS:
+        Y[row_base + tid] = S.convert(row_max[tid], S.bf16)
+
+
+class ModelNew(nn.Module):
     def __init__(self, in_features, out_features, pool_kernel_size, scale_factor):
         super().__init__()
         self.matmul = nn.Linear(in_features, out_features)
         self.avg_pool = nn.AvgPool1d(kernel_size=pool_kernel_size)
         self.scale_factor = scale_factor
+        self._cached_weight = None
+        self._cached_bias = None
+        self._cache_key = None
 
+    def _get_cached_params(self, x: torch.Tensor):
+        weight = self.matmul.weight
+        bias = self.matmul.bias
+        key = (
+            weight.data_ptr(),
+            bias.data_ptr(),
+            x.device,
+            x.dtype,
+        )
+        if self._cache_key != key:
+            self._cached_weight = weight.t().to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
+            self._cached_bias = bias.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
+            self._cache_key = key
+        return self._cached_weight, self._cached_bias
+

+import torch
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+M = 64
+N = 64
+K = 16
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def test_kernel(A: S.Tensor((M, K), S.bf16), B: S.Tensor((N, K), S.bf16), C: S.Tensor((M, N), S.f32)):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // 64
+    lane = tid % 64
+    warp_row = warp_id // 2
+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+    lane_lo = lane % 32
+    lane_hi = lane // 32
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, S.convert(M * K * 2, S.i32))
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B, S.convert(K * N * 2, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    a_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    c_tile = S.make_shared((M, N), S.f32)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    if tid < 128:
+        load_idx = tid
+        load_row = load_idx % 64
+        seg = load_idx // 64
+        a_row_block = load_row // 32
+        a_row_lane = load_row % 32
+        a_off = S.convert((load_row * K + seg * 8) * 2, S.i32)
+        x_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_off, 0)
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane, seg * 2 + 0] = x_pack[0]
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane, seg * 2 + 1] = x_pack[1]
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 0] = x_pack[2]
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 1] = x_pack[3]
+    else:
+        load_idx = tid - 128
+        load_col = load_idx % 64
+        seg = load_idx // 64
+        b_col_block = load_col // 32
+        b_col_lane = load_col % 32
+        b_off = S.convert((load_col * K + seg * 8) * 2, S.i32)
+        w_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_off, 0)
+        b_words[b_col_block, b_col_lane, seg * 2 + 0] = w_pack[0]
+        b_words[b_col_block, b_col_lane, seg * 2 + 1] = w_pack[1]
+        b_words[b_col_block, b_col_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 0] = w_pack[2]
+        b_words[b_col_block, b_col_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 1] = w_pack[3]
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    m_a = S.view(a_words[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(b_words[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)
+
+    local_col = warp_col * 32 + lane_lo
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        local_row = warp_row * 32 + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_hi + (acc_idx % 4)
+        c_tile[local_row, local_col] = c_lane[acc_idx]
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if tid < 64:
+        for j in S.range(64):
+            C[tid, j] = c_tile[tid, j]
+
+
+def main():
+    torch.manual_seed(0)
+    A = torch.randn((M, K), device="cuda", dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+    B = torch.randn((K, N), device="cuda", dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+    B_t = B.t().contiguous()
+    C = torch.zeros((M, N), device="cuda", dtype=torch.float32)
+    test_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (256, 1, 1))](A, B_t, C)
+    ref = A.float() @ B.float()
+    d = (C - ref).abs()
+    print("max", d.max().item(), "mean", d.mean().item())
+    print("row0_ref", ref[0, :16].cpu().tolist())
+    print("row0_got", C[0, :16].cpu().tolist())
+    print("row1_ref", ref[1, :16].cpu().tolist())
+    print("row1_got", C[1, :16].cpu().tolist())
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+            self._cached_bias = bias.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
+            self._cache_key = key

+import torch
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+M = 64
+N = 64
+K = 16
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def test_kernel(A: S.Tensor((M, K), S.bf16), B: S.Tensor((N, K), S.bf16), C: S.Tensor((M, N), S.f32)):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // 64
+    lane = tid % 64
+    warp_row = warp_id // 2
+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+    lane_lo = lane % 32
+    lane_hi = lane // 32
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, S.convert(M * K * 2, S.i32))
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B, S.convert(K * N * 2, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    a_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    c_tile = S.make_shared((M, N), S.f32)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    if tid < 128:
+        load_idx = tid
+        load_row = load_idx % 64
+        seg = load_idx // 64
+        a_row_block = load_row // 32
+        a_row_lane = load_row % 32
+        a_off = S.convert((load_row * K + seg * 8) * 2, S.i32)
+        x_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_off, 0)
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane, seg * 2 + 0] = x_pack[0]
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane, seg * 2 + 1] = x_pack[1]
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 0] = x_pack[2]
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 1] = x_pack[3]
+    else:
+        load_idx = tid - 128
+        load_col = load_idx % 64
+        seg = load_idx // 64
+        b_col_block = load_col // 32
+        b_col_lane = load_col % 32
+        b_off = S.convert((load_col * K + seg * 8) * 2, S.i32)
+        w_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_off, 0)
+        b_words[b_col_block, b_col_lane, seg * 2 + 0] = w_pack[0]
+        b_words[b_col_block, b_col_lane, seg * 2 + 1] = w_pack[1]
+        b_words[b_col_block, b_col_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 0] = w_pack[2]
+        b_words[b_col_block, b_col_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 1] = w_pack[3]
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    m_a = S.view(a_words[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(b_words[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)
+
+    local_col = warp_col * 32 + lane_lo
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        local_row = warp_row * 32 + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_hi + (acc_idx % 4)
+        c_tile[local_row, local_col] = c_lane[acc_idx]
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if tid < 64:
+        for j in S.range(64):
+            C[tid, j] = c_tile[tid, j]
+
+
+def main():
+    torch.manual_seed(0)
+    A = torch.randn((M, K), device="cuda", dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+    B = torch.randn((K, N), device="cuda", dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+    B_t = B.t().contiguous()
+    C = torch.zeros((M, N), device="cuda", dtype=torch.float32)
+    test_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (256, 1, 1))](A, B_t, C)
+    ref = A.float() @ B.float()
+    d = (C - ref).abs()
+    print("max", d.max().item(), "mean", d.mean().item())
+    print("row0_ref", ref[0, :16].cpu().tolist())
+    print("row0_got", C[0, :16].cpu().tolist())
+    print("row1_ref", ref[1, :16].cpu().tolist())
+    print("row1_got", C[1, :16].cpu().tolist())
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+            C[tid, j] = c_tile[tid, j]
+
+

+    torch.manual_seed(0)
+    A = torch.randn((M, K), device="cuda", dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+    B = torch.randn((K, N), device="cuda", dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+    B_t = B.t().contiguous()
+    C = torch.zeros((M, N), device="cuda", dtype=torch.float32)
+    test_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (256, 1, 1))](A, B_t, C)
+    ref = A.float() @ B.float()
+    d = (C - ref).abs()

+    print("row1_ref", ref[1, :16].cpu().tolist())
+    print("row1_got", C[1, :16].cpu().tolist())
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp_id // 2
+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+    lane_lo = lane % 32
+    lane_hi = lane // 32
+    row_block = S.block_id(0)
+    row_base = row_block * BLOCK_ROWS

+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_words = S.make_shared((2, WAVE_SIZE, 4), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((2, WAVE_SIZE, 4), S.u32)
+    c_tile = S.make_shared((BLOCK_ROWS, BLOCK_COLS), S.f32)
+    row_max = S.make_shared((BLOCK_ROWS,), S.f32)
+

+    if tid < BLOCK_ROWS:
+        row_max[tid] = neg_inf
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    for col_tile in S.range(COL_TILES):

+            if tid < 128:

+                a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 0] = x_pack[2]

+            self._cached_bias = bias.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()

+import torch
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+M = 64
+N = 64
+K = 16
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def test_kernel(A: S.Tensor((M, K), S.bf16), B: S.Tensor((N, K), S.bf16), C: S.Tensor((M, N), S.f32)):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // 64
+    lane = tid % 64
+    warp_row = warp_id // 2
+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+    lane_lo = lane % 32
+    lane_hi = lane // 32
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, S.convert(M * K * 2, S.i32))
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B, S.convert(K * N * 2, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    a_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    c_tile = S.make_shared((M, N), S.f32)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    if tid < 128:
+        load_idx = tid
+        load_row = load_idx % 64
+        seg = load_idx // 64
+        a_row_block = load_row // 32
+        a_row_lane = load_row % 32
+        a_off = S.convert((load_row * K + seg * 8) * 2, S.i32)
+        x_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_off, 0)
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane, seg * 2 + 0] = x_pack[0]
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane, seg * 2 + 1] = x_pack[1]
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 0] = x_pack[2]
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 1] = x_pack[3]
+    else:
+        load_idx = tid - 128
+        load_col = load_idx % 64
+        seg = load_idx // 64
+        b_col_block = load_col // 32
+        b_col_lane = load_col % 32
+        b_off = S.convert((load_col * K + seg * 8) * 2, S.i32)
+        w_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_off, 0)
+        b_words[b_col_block, b_col_lane, seg * 2 + 0] = w_pack[0]
+        b_words[b_col_block, b_col_lane, seg * 2 + 1] = w_pack[1]
+        b_words[b_col_block, b_col_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 0] = w_pack[2]
+        b_words[b_col_block, b_col_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 1] = w_pack[3]
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    m_a = S.view(a_words[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(b_words[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)
+
+    local_col = warp_col * 32 + lane_lo
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        local_row = warp_row * 32 + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_hi + (acc_idx % 4)
+        c_tile[local_row, local_col] = c_lane[acc_idx]
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if tid < 64:
+        for j in S.range(64):
+            C[tid, j] = c_tile[tid, j]
+
+
+def main():
+    torch.manual_seed(0)
+    A = torch.randn((M, K), device="cuda", dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+    B = torch.randn((K, N), device="cuda", dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+    B_t = B.t().contiguous()
+    C = torch.zeros((M, N), device="cuda", dtype=torch.float32)
+    test_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (256, 1, 1))](A, B_t, C)
+    ref = A.float() @ B.float()
+    d = (C - ref).abs()
+    print("max", d.max().item(), "mean", d.mean().item())
+    print("row0_ref", ref[0, :16].cpu().tolist())
+    print("row0_got", C[0, :16].cpu().tolist())
+    print("row1_ref", ref[1, :16].cpu().tolist())
+    print("row1_got", C[1, :16].cpu().tolist())
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+            m_b = S.view(b_words[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+            c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+            c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)
+            S.syncthreads()
+
+        local_col = warp_col * 32 + lane_lo
+        for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+            local_row = warp_row * 32 + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_hi + (acc_idx % 4)
+            c_tile[local_row, local_col] = c_lane[acc_idx]
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        if tid < BLOCK_ROWS:
+            row = tid
+            for group in S.range(BLOCK_COLS // POOL_KERNEL_SIZE):
+                total = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+                group_col = col_base + group * POOL_KERNEL_SIZE
+                for t in S.range(POOL_KERNEL_SIZE):
+                    col = group * POOL_KERNEL_SIZE + t
+                    total += c_tile[row, col] + S.convert(BIAS0[group_col + t], S.f32)
+                v = total / S.convert(POOL_KERNEL_SIZE, S.f32)
+                v = S.convert(0.5, S.f32) * v * (
+                    S.convert(1.0, S.f32) + S.erf(v / S.convert(SQRT_2, S.f32))
+                )
+                v = v * S.convert(SCALE_FACTOR, S.f32)
+                if v > row_max[row]:
+                    row_max[row] = v
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    if tid < BLOCK_ROWS:
+        Y[row_base + tid] = S.convert(row_max[tid], S.bf16)
+
+
+class ModelNew(nn.Module):
     def __init__(self, in_features, out_features, pool_kernel_size, scale_factor):
         super().__init__()
         self.matmul = nn.Linear(in_features, out_features)
         self.avg_pool = nn.AvgPool1d(kernel_size=pool_kernel_size)
         self.scale_factor = scale_factor
+        self._cached_weight = None
+        self._cached_bias = None
+        self._cache_key = None
+
+    def _get_cached_params(self, x: torch.Tensor):
+        weight = self.matmul.weight
+        bias = self.matmul.bias
+        key = (
+            weight.data_ptr(),
+            bias.data_ptr(),
+            x.device,
+            x.dtype,
+        )
+        if self._cache_key != key:
+            self._cached_weight = weight.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
+            self._cached_bias = bias.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
+            self._cache_key = key
+        return self._cached_weight, self._cached_bias
 
     def forward(self, x):
-        if tuple(x.shape) != (BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES) or x.dtype != torch.bfloat16 or self.avg_pool.kernel_size != POOL_KERNEL_SIZE or (self.scale_factor != SCALE_FACTOR):
-            raise RuntimeError('This fused kernel only supports the benchmark input shape and dtype.')

-        bias = self.matmul.bias.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()

+import torch
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+M = 64
+N = 64
+K = 16
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def test_kernel(A: S.Tensor((M, K), S.bf16), B: S.Tensor((N, K), S.bf16), C: S.Tensor((M, N), S.f32)):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // 64
+    lane = tid % 64
+    warp_row = warp_id // 2
+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+    lane_lo = lane % 32
+    lane_hi = lane // 32
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, S.convert(M * K * 2, S.i32))
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B, S.convert(K * N * 2, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    a_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    c_tile = S.make_shared((M, N), S.f32)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    if tid < 128:
+        load_idx = tid
+        load_row = load_idx % 64
+        seg = load_idx // 64
+        a_row_block = load_row // 32
+        a_row_lane = load_row % 32
+        a_off = S.convert((load_row * K + seg * 8) * 2, S.i32)
+        x_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_off, 0)
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane, seg * 2 + 0] = x_pack[0]
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane, seg * 2 + 1] = x_pack[1]
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 0] = x_pack[2]
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 1] = x_pack[3]
+    else:
+        load_idx = tid - 128
+        load_col = load_idx % 64
+        seg = load_idx // 64
+        b_col_block = load_col // 32
+        b_col_lane = load_col % 32
+        b_off = S.convert((load_col * K + seg * 8) * 2, S.i32)
+        w_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_off, 0)
+        b_words[b_col_block, b_col_lane, seg * 2 + 0] = w_pack[0]
+        b_words[b_col_block, b_col_lane, seg * 2 + 1] = w_pack[1]
+        b_words[b_col_block, b_col_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 0] = w_pack[2]
+        b_words[b_col_block, b_col_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 1] = w_pack[3]
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    m_a = S.view(a_words[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(b_words[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)
+
+    local_col = warp_col * 32 + lane_lo
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        local_row = warp_row * 32 + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_hi + (acc_idx % 4)
+        c_tile[local_row, local_col] = c_lane[acc_idx]
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if tid < 64:
+        for j in S.range(64):
+            C[tid, j] = c_tile[tid, j]
+
+
+def main():
+    torch.manual_seed(0)
+    A = torch.randn((M, K), device="cuda", dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+    B = torch.randn((K, N), device="cuda", dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+    B_t = B.t().contiguous()
+    C = torch.zeros((M, N), device="cuda", dtype=torch.float32)
+    test_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (256, 1, 1))](A, B_t, C)
+    ref = A.float() @ B.float()
+    d = (C - ref).abs()
+    print("max", d.max().item(), "mean", d.mean().item())
+    print("row0_ref", ref[0, :16].cpu().tolist())
+    print("row0_got", C[0, :16].cpu().tolist())
+    print("row1_ref", ref[1, :16].cpu().tolist())
+    print("row1_got", C[1, :16].cpu().tolist())
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+import torch
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+M = 64
+N = 64
+K = 16
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def test_kernel(A: S.Tensor((M, K), S.bf16), B: S.Tensor((N, K), S.bf16), C: S.Tensor((M, N), S.f32)):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // 64
+    lane = tid % 64
+    warp_row = warp_id // 2
+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+    lane_lo = lane % 32
+    lane_hi = lane // 32
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, S.convert(M * K * 2, S.i32))
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B, S.convert(K * N * 2, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    a_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    c_tile = S.make_shared((M, N), S.f32)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    if tid < 128:
+        load_idx = tid
+        load_row = load_idx % 64
+        seg = load_idx // 64
+        a_row_block = load_row // 32
+        a_row_lane = load_row % 32
+        a_off = S.convert((load_row * K + seg * 8) * 2, S.i32)
+        x_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_off, 0)
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane, seg * 2 + 0] = x_pack[0]
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane, seg * 2 + 1] = x_pack[1]
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 0] = x_pack[2]
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 1] = x_pack[3]
+    else:
+        load_idx = tid - 128
+        load_col = load_idx % 64
+        seg = load_idx // 64
+        b_col_block = load_col // 32
+        b_col_lane = load_col % 32
+        b_off = S.convert((load_col * K + seg * 8) * 2, S.i32)
+        w_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_off, 0)
+        b_words[b_col_block, b_col_lane, seg * 2 + 0] = w_pack[0]
+        b_words[b_col_block, b_col_lane, seg * 2 + 1] = w_pack[1]
+        b_words[b_col_block, b_col_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 0] = w_pack[2]
+        b_words[b_col_block, b_col_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 1] = w_pack[3]
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    m_a = S.view(a_words[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(b_words[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)
+
+    local_col = warp_col * 32 + lane_lo
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        local_row = warp_row * 32 + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_hi + (acc_idx % 4)
+        c_tile[local_row, local_col] = c_lane[acc_idx]
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if tid < 64:
+        for j in S.range(64):
+            C[tid, j] = c_tile[tid, j]
+
+
+def main():
+    torch.manual_seed(0)
+    A = torch.randn((M, K), device="cuda", dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+    B = torch.randn((K, N), device="cuda", dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+    B_t = B.t().contiguous()
+    C = torch.zeros((M, N), device="cuda", dtype=torch.float32)
+    test_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (256, 1, 1))](A, B_t, C)
+    ref = A.float() @ B.float()
+    d = (C - ref).abs()
+    print("max", d.max().item(), "mean", d.mean().item())
+    print("row0_ref", ref[0, :16].cpu().tolist())
+    print("row0_got", C[0, :16].cpu().tolist())
+    print("row1_ref", ref[1, :16].cpu().tolist())
+    print("row1_got", C[1, :16].cpu().tolist())
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp_id // 2
+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+    lane_lo = lane % 32
+    lane_hi = lane // 32
+    row_block = S.block_id(0)
+    row_base = row_block * BLOCK_ROWS

+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_words = S.make_shared((2, WAVE_SIZE, 4), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((2, WAVE_SIZE, 4), S.u32)
+    c_tile = S.make_shared((BLOCK_ROWS, BLOCK_COLS), S.f32)
+    row_max = S.make_shared((BLOCK_ROWS,), S.f32)
+
+    neg_inf = S.convert(-1.0e30, S.f32)
+    if tid < BLOCK_ROWS:
+        row_max[tid] = neg_inf
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    for col_tile in S.range(COL_TILES):
+        c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+        col_base = col_tile * BLOCK_COLS

+        for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+            k_base = k_tile * BLOCK_K
+
+            if tid < 128:
+                load_idx = tid
+                load_row = load_idx % BLOCK_ROWS
+                seg = load_idx // BLOCK_ROWS

+                a_row_lane = load_row % 32
+                x_row = row_base + load_row

+                x_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, x_off, 0)

+                a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane, seg * 2 + 1] = x_pack[1]
+                a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 0] = x_pack[2]
+                a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 1] = x_pack[3]

+import torch
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+M = 64
+N = 64
+K = 16
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def test_kernel(A: S.Tensor((M, K), S.bf16), B: S.Tensor((N, K), S.bf16), C: S.Tensor((M, N), S.f32)):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // 64
+    lane = tid % 64
+    warp_row = warp_id // 2
+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+    lane_lo = lane % 32
+    lane_hi = lane // 32
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, S.convert(M * K * 2, S.i32))
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B, S.convert(K * N * 2, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    a_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    c_tile = S.make_shared((M, N), S.f32)
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    if tid < 128:
+        load_idx = tid
+        load_row = load_idx % 64
+        seg = load_idx // 64
+        a_row_block = load_row // 32
+        a_row_lane = load_row % 32
+        a_off = S.convert((load_row * K + seg * 8) * 2, S.i32)
+        x_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_off, 0)
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane, seg * 2 + 0] = x_pack[0]
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane, seg * 2 + 1] = x_pack[1]
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 0] = x_pack[2]
+        a_words[a_row_block, a_row_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 1] = x_pack[3]
+    else:
+        load_idx = tid - 128
+        load_col = load_idx % 64
+        seg = load_idx // 64
+        b_col_block = load_col // 32
+        b_col_lane = load_col % 32
+        b_off = S.convert((load_col * K + seg * 8) * 2, S.i32)
+        w_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_off, 0)
+        b_words[b_col_block, b_col_lane, seg * 2 + 0] = w_pack[0]
+        b_words[b_col_block, b_col_lane, seg * 2 + 1] = w_pack[1]
+        b_words[b_col_block, b_col_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 0] = w_pack[2]
+        b_words[b_col_block, b_col_lane + 32, seg * 2 + 1] = w_pack[3]
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    m_a = S.view(a_words[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    m_b = S.view(b_words[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)
+
+    local_col = warp_col * 32 + lane_lo
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        local_row = warp_row * 32 + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_hi + (acc_idx % 4)
+        c_tile[local_row, local_col] = c_lane[acc_idx]
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if tid < 64:
+        for j in S.range(64):
+            C[tid, j] = c_tile[tid, j]
+
+
+def main():
+    torch.manual_seed(0)
+    A = torch.randn((M, K), device="cuda", dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+    B = torch.randn((K, N), device="cuda", dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+    B_t = B.t().contiguous()
+    C = torch.zeros((M, N), device="cuda", dtype=torch.float32)
+    test_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (256, 1, 1))](A, B_t, C)
+    ref = A.float() @ B.float()
+    d = (C - ref).abs()
+    print("max", d.max().item(), "mean", d.mean().item())
+    print("row0_ref", ref[0, :16].cpu().tolist())
+    print("row0_got", C[0, :16].cpu().tolist())
+    print("row1_ref", ref[1, :16].cpu().tolist())
+    print("row1_got", C[1, :16].cpu().tolist())
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE,), S.bf16),

+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    warp_id = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp_id // 2
+    warp_col = warp_id % 2
+    lane_lo = lane % 32
+    lane_hi = lane // 32
+    row_block = S.block_id(0)
+    row_base = row_block * BLOCK_ROWS

+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(W_NUM_BYTES, S.i32))
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    a_words = S.make_shared((2, WAVE_SIZE, 4), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((2, WAVE_SIZE, 4), S.u32)
+    c_tile = S.make_shared((BLOCK_ROWS, BLOCK_COLS), S.f32)

+    if tid < BLOCK_ROWS:

+    S.syncthreads()
+

+        col_base = col_tile * BLOCK_COLS

+            if tid < 128:

+                load_row = load_idx % BLOCK_ROWS

+                a_row_lane = load_row % 32

codex
Implemented the optimized MFMA-based fused kernel in [output_model_new.py](/workspace/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb2/p98/optimization_rounds/round1/output_model_new.py). It now uses 4 waves as a 2x2 warp grid, stages operands through LDS, issues `S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32`, uses `S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4`, and keeps the fused pool/GELU/max reduction in the kernel. I also made the weight/bias path cudagraph-safe by caching the device/dtype-converted tensors and only rebuilding on storage-pointer changes.

Validation passed with the required harness command. The latest round-local result in `debug_eval.jsonl` reports `correctness: true` and `runtime_us: 180.0`.
